[30;1m117 | [0m[35m## Version-String Flavors[0m
[30;1m118 | [0m[35m[0m
[30;1m119 | [0m[35mCode which uses Versioneer can learn about its version string at runtime by[0m

[30;1m121 | [0m[35m`get_versions()` function. From the "outside" (e.g. in `setup.py`), you can[0m
[30;1m122 | [0m[35mimport the top-level `versioneer.py` and run `get_versions()`.[0m
